FROM (
	  SELECT DISTINCT v1."nr" AS "nr2m23", v6."productfeature" AS "productfeature2m2"
	  FROM "ss1"."product1" v1, "ss1"."productfeatureproduct1" v6
	  WHERE v1."nr" <= 2 AND v1."nr"=v6."product"
	  UNION ALL
	  SELECT DISTINCT v3."nr" AS "nr2m23", v8."productfeature" AS "productfeature2m2"
	  FROM "ss5"."product2" v3, "ss5"."productfeatureproduct2" v8
	  WHERE v3."nr" <= 2 AND v3."nr"=v8."product"
    ) v12
GROUP BY v12."nr2m23"

            WHERE ((v1."nr" IS NOT NULL AND v1."label" IS NOT NULL) AND (v1."nr" <> 7) AND (v1."nr"=v11."product")

            FROM "ss5"."product2" v3, "ss5"."productfeatureproduct2" v13

                  WHERE 7 = v8."product"
                 ) v10, (
						 SELECT v16."propertynum1" AS "propertynum1m41"

                         WHERE (v16."propertynum1" IS NOT NULL AND 7 = v16."nr")
                         UNION ALL
                         SELECT v18."propertynum1" AS "propertynum1m41"
                         FROM "ss5"."product2" v18
                         WHERE (v18."propertynum1" IS NOT NULL AND 7 = v18."nr")
                        ) v20, (

                                FROM "ss5"."product2" v28

              v10."productfeature2m2" = v5."productfeature2m1")
